### [192] [Novel exact solutions of the Duffing equation: stability analysis and application to real non-linear deformation tests](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.24774)
*A. D. Berezner,V. A. Fedorov,N. S. Perov,G. V. Grigoriev*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本研究提出了Duffing方程的新精确解及其相图，揭示了参数增长导致相轨迹从椭圆变为不稳定区域的畸变，并通过傅里叶级数分析确定了不稳定性判据。研究还推导了对应微分算子的显式形式，并成功应用于非等温蠕变行为及铁磁非晶合金在非线性变形下热-磁性能关系的描述，模型与实验具有高线性相关性，可准确预测有机和金属系统在介观尺度的力学行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了更准确地描述非线性动力学系统（如Duffing方程）在复杂条件下的行为，特别是材料在非等温蠕变和非线性变形中的响应，研究旨在发展新的精确解并建立其物理诠释，以揭示不稳定性机制并关联多场耦合性质。

Method: 采用解析方法求解Duffing方程，获得新的精确解并绘制相图；利用傅里叶级数变换分析解的谐波成分；推导对应的微分算子并评估其功能谱；将所得解应用于非等温蠕变实验数据拟合，并结合临界指数分析铁磁非晶合金的热-磁耦合特性。

Result: 获得了Duffing方程的新精确解，发现相轨迹随参数变化由椭圆逐渐畸变至不稳定状态；明确了不稳定性的判据；得到了微分算子的显式表达及其谱特性；成功用该模型描述多种材料的非等温蠕变直至断裂过程；实验验证显示模型与有机及金属系统的实测数据具有高线性相关性，且能有效预测介观尺度下的热-力-磁耦合行为。

Conclusion: 所提出的Duffing方程新解及其分析方法为理解非线性动力系统中的不稳定现象提供了理论基础，并在材料科学中展现出广泛应用潜力，特别是在非等温非线性变形过程中多物理场耦合行为的建模与预测方面表现优异。

Abstract: In this study, novel exact solutions of the Duffing equation with their phase portraits have been proposed and reasoned. It is shown that phase trajectories are initially elliptical and become distorted in the unstable area within the growth of the variable parameter. Instability criteria of identified solutions have been determined together with the Fourier series transformation up to the first and high harmonics in a sense of the physical interpretation. An explicit form for the differential operator, corresponding to considered functions, has been derived with evaluation of its main functional spectrum. Non-isothermal creep tests of different materials were completely described using the Duffing equation via noted solutions up to the fracture as processes with personal deformation response. We successfully examined a relationship between the thermal and magnetic properties of the ferromagnetic amorphous alloy under its non-linear deformation, using the critical exponents. With a high linear correlation between our model and experiments, behaviour of organic and metallic systems is well predicted at the same thermo-mechanical testing conditions on the mesoscale.

</details>


### [193] [Graphicality of power-law and double power-law degree sequences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.24976)
*Pietro Valigi,M. Ángeles Serrano,Claudio Castellano,Lorenzo Cirigliano*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 研究了幂律分布和双幂律分布度序列的图化性问题，结合精确条件与启发式条件，揭示了不同类型序列不可图化的物理机制，并通过数值分析验证了理论结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨具有尺寸依赖截断的幂律分布和具有尺寸依赖交叉的双幂律分布度序列的图化性，理解其在有限尺寸下与无限尺寸极限之间的差异及其背后的物理原因。

Method: 结合使用图化性的精确充分条件和非图化性的启发式条件，辅以广泛的数值分析。

Result: 对于单个幂律恢复了已知的相图，阐明了不同机制之间微妙的相互作用；对于双幂律推导出所有可能指数组合下的图化性，发现五种本质上不同的非图化方式。

Conclusion: 揭示了双幂律度序列图化性的丰富相图及多种非图化机制，解释了某些情况下有限系统与无限系统行为的巨大差异。

Abstract: The graphicality problem -- whether or not a sequence of integers can be used to create a simple graph -- is a key question in network theory and combinatorics, with many important practical applications. In this work, we study the graphicality of degree sequences distributed as a power-law with a size-dependent cutoff and as a double power-law with a size-dependent crossover. We combine the application of exact sufficient conditions for graphicality with heuristic conditions for nongraphicality which allow us to elucidate the physical reasons why some sequences are not graphical. For single power-laws we recover the known phase-diagram, we highlight the subtle interplay of distinct mechanisms violating graphicality and we explain why the infinite-size limit behavior is in some cases very far from being observed for finite sequences. For double power-laws we derive the graphicality of infinite sequences for all possible values of the degree exponents $γ_1$ and $γ_2$, uncovering a rich phase-diagram and pointing out the existence of five qualitatively distinct ways graphicality can be violated. The validity of theoretical arguments is supported by extensive numerical analysis.

</details>

### [194] [Wind Speed Weibull Model Identification in Oman, and Computed Normalized Annual Energy Production (NAEP) From Wind Turbines Based on Data From Weather Stations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.23715)
*Osama A. Marzouk*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本研究基于阿曼2000至2023年的气象站风速观测数据，利用威布尔分布模型分析10个站点的风能潜力，并评估归一化年发电量（NAEP）及主导风向。结果显示Thumrait风速最高且风向稳定，是最适宜建设大型风电场的地点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为评估阿曼各地风能资源潜力，支持可再生能源开发决策，特别是识别适合建设大规模风电场的最优地理位置。

Method: 采用威布尔分布的形状和尺度参数对10个气象站的风速数据进行建模，计算超过6 m/s风速的概率，并估算每兆瓦装机容量的归一化年发电量（NAEP），同时统计分析风向分布。

Result: 四个地点风能资源显著优于其他地区：Thumrait、Masirah、Sur和Fahud。其中Thumrait的风速超过6 m/s的概率达41.71%，NAEP为1.727 GWh/MWp/年，风向高度集中于南东南（SSE）方向。

Conclusion: Thumrait因其高风速、高单向性和优越地理条件，成为阿曼最适宜建设 utility-scale 风电场的候选地，具备显著的风能开发潜力。

Abstract: Using observation records of wind speeds from weather stations in the Sultanate of Oman between 2000 and 2023, we compute estimators of the two Weibull distribution parameters (namely, the Weibull distribution's shape parameter and the Weibull distribution's scale parameter) in 10 weather station locations within eight Omani governorates. The 10 weather station locations in Oman and their corresponding governorates are Seeb (in Muscat), Salalah (in Dhofar), Buraimi (in Al Buraimi), Masirah (in Ash Sharqiyah South), Thumrait (in Dhofar), Sur (in Ash Sharqiyah South), Khasab (in Musandam), Sohar (in Sohar), Fahud (in Az Zahirah), and Saiq (in Ad Dakhiliyah). The obtained wind speed distributions at these weather stations are then used to predict the annual energy production (AEP) for a proposed reference amount of 1 MWp of wind turbine capacity, and this specific AEP is designated here by the term "normalized annual energy production (NAEP)." The direction of the wind is also analyzed statistically over the same period to identify the more probable wind directions. Four locations were clearly distinguishable as being windy compared to the others. The simulated probability of exceeding a feasible 6 m/s (21.6 km/h) wind speed in these locations is 41.71% in Thumrait, 37.77% in Masirah, 29.53% in Sur, and 17.03% in Fahud. The NAEP values in these four locations are estimated as 1.727 GWh/MWp/year, 1.419 GWh/MWp/year, 1.038 GWh/MWp/year, and 0.602 GWh/MWp/year, respectively. The wind in the location of Thumrait is not only the fastest (on average) among the selected locations but also the most unidirectional, blowing almost always from the south-south-east (SSE) direction, and both features make this non-coastal location in southern Oman, with an altitude of about 467 m, an attractive site for utility-scale wind farms.

</details>


### [195] [A Survey of AI Methods for Geometry Preparation and Mesh Generation in Engineering Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.23719)
*Steven Owen,Nathan Brown,Nikos Chrisochoides,Rao Garimella,Xianfeng Gu,Franck Ledoux,Na Lei,Roshan Quadros,Navamita Ray,Nicolas Winovich,Yongjie Jessica Zhang*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 该论文综述了人工智能在CAD到网格生成流程中的应用进展，重点涵盖零件分类、网格质量预测、去特征化及网格生成的改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决传统CAD到网格转换过程中长期存在的瓶颈问题，提升自动化和效率。

Method: 综述机器学习在非结构化与块结构化网格生成、体参数化、并行网格生成加速以及脚本自动化（如强化学习和大语言模型）中的应用。

Result: AI作为辅助技术，增强了传统几何与网格工具的能力，已在多个环节实现实际部署。

Conclusion: AI正在推动数据驱动的下一代网格工作流发展，但仍面临关键研究挑战。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence is beginning to ease long-standing bottlenecks in the CAD-to-mesh pipeline. This survey reviews recent advances where machine learning aids part classification, mesh quality prediction, and defeaturing. We explore methods that improve unstructured and block-structured meshing, support volumetric parameterizations, and accelerate parallel mesh generation. We also examine emerging tools for scripting automation, including reinforcement learning and large language models. Across these efforts, AI acts as an assistive technology, extending the capabilities of traditional geometry and meshing tools. The survey highlights representative methods, practical deployments, and key research challenges that will shape the next generation of data-driven meshing workflows.

</details>
